Résumé du jour

Airbus uses artificial intelligence for various applications, including predictive maintenance and contract analysis, but does not rely on AI to design aircraft. The company employs a dedicated team for AI and advanced analytics. Airbus Helicopters has invested in new facilities for transmission assembly.
